End-to-end QSA+DEA
Each run generates the QSA field→question mapping fresh, feeds it (with the conversation, NOT the location prompt) to the production DEA prompt. The LLM judge scores ONLY the conversation vs. what the DEA extracted (which fields were mapped, which were missed). Separately, a non-LLM check on the raw QSA output counts how often it came back empty or hallucinated (repeated itself). Treat the judge's score as a signal, not ground truth — every run shows the conversation, mapping, and extraction so you can check it yourself.

DEA prompt
You are a data extraction agent. You are given a conversation between a user and an assistant. You need to extract the data from the conversation.

## Questions Mapping from the user's System prompt:
```markdown
| Field Name         | Questions                                                                                   |
|--------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Reason for Contact  | Are you reaching out about vehicle service, or about buying/financing a car?; What brings you in today on the buying side? |
| VIN                | Could you share your VIN so we can pull the right specs?                                   |
| Service Needed     | What seems to be going on with the vehicle, or what service are you after?                  |
| Preferred Drop-off Day | What day were you hoping to drop it off?                                                  |
| full_name          | Whose name is the appointment under?; Can I get your full name for the application?        |
| phone              | And the best phone number to text you a confirmation?; What's the best phone number to reach you? |
| email              | And an email address to send the pre-approval to?                                          |
| Annual Income      | Roughly what do you bring in per year before taxes?                                        |
```

### Conversation:
User: "My car is making a grinding noise and I think I need it looked at."
---
Assistant: "Are you reaching out about vehicle service, or about buying/financing a car?"
---
User: "Vehicle service please."
---
Assistant: "Got it. What seems to be going on with the vehicle, or what service are you after?"
---
User: "There's a grinding sound when I brake, so I think I need a brake inspection and probably new pads."
---
Assistant: "Thanks. Could you share your VIN so we can pull the right specs?"
---
User: "Sure, it's 1HGCM82633A004352."
---
Assistant: "Perfect, that helps us pull the right parts. What day were you hoping to drop it off?"
---
User: "This Saturday would be ideal."
---
Assistant: "Great, Saturday works. A service advisor will follow up to confirm your brake inspection appointment. Thanks for choosing Cornerstone Auto!"

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.


 ### Tools Available:
- * data_extraction_custom: Extract the data for the custom fields as per the field description
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.
### When to Use Tools:
- * data_extraction_custom: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around custom fields
Example for data_extraction_custom: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked around 'Why the customer is reaching out (service vs purchase/finance).', user provided their information similar to [\"Need an oil change\",\"Looking to finance a car\"], that is valid and extracted","data_extracted":[{"unique_id":"cf_reason","data":"Need an oil change"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

User: "I'd say mild, it's annoying but manageable."

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools

## Questions Mapping from the user's System prompt:
| Field Name               | Questions                                                                                                  |
|--------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Issue Description        | Can you tell me what's happening?                                                                          |
| Emergency Status         | Is this an emergency that needs someone today, or can it wait for a scheduled visit?                        |
| Service Address          | What's the address we're coming to?; What's the address for the visit?                                     |
| Service Area             | Which town or area is that in?; What town or area is that?                                                 |
| Preferred Appointment Window | What time window works best for you?                                                                     |
| postal_code              | What's your ZIP code so we can confirm you're in our coverage?                                             |
| full_name                | And whose name should the appointment be under?                                                           |
| phone                   | What's the best cell number in case the tech needs to call on the way?                                     |

### Conversation:
User: "It's 42 Elm Street, the clog is in the kitchen on the first floor."
---
Assistant: "Thanks. What town or area is that?"
---
User: "That's in Bellevue."
---
Assistant: "Perfect. What time window works best for you?"
---
User: "Tomorrow morning would be great."
---
Assistant: "Got it. What's your ZIP code so we can confirm you're in our coverage?"
---
User: "98004"
---
Assistant: "And whose name should the appointment be under?"
---
User: "Put it under Marcus."
---
Assistant: "All set, Marcus. We'll confirm your tomorrow-morning window shortly. Thanks for calling BlueFlame!"

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.


 ### Tools Available:
- * data_extraction_standard: Extract the data for the standard fields as per the field description
- * data_extraction_custom: Extract the data for the custom fields as per the field description
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.
### When to Use Tools:
- * data_extraction_standard: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around standard fields
Example for data_extraction_standard: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked for postal_code, user provided their information, which is valid and hence extracted","data_extracted":[{"field_name":"postal_code","data":"90210"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * data_extraction_custom: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around custom fields
Example for data_extraction_custom: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked around 'What is going wrong (leak, no heat, clog, etc.).', user provided their information similar to [\"Water heater leaking\",\"Furnace won't start\"], that is valid and extracted","data_extracted":[{"unique_id":"cf_issue","data":"Water heater leaking"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.


 ### Tools Available:
- * data_extraction_custom: Extract the data for the custom fields as per the field description
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.
### When to Use Tools:
- * data_extraction_custom: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around custom fields
Example for data_extraction_custom: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked around 'Whether the caller is a new or existing patient.', user provided their information similar to [\"New patient\",\"Returning\"], that is valid and extracted","data_extracted":[{"unique_id":"cf_patient_type","data":"New patient"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.


 ### Tools Available:
- * data_extraction_standard: Extract the data for the standard fields as per the field description
- * data_extraction_custom: Extract the data for the custom fields as per the field description
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.
### When to Use Tools:
- * data_extraction_standard: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around standard fields
Example for data_extraction_standard: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked for postal_code, user provided their information, which is valid and hence extracted","data_extracted":[{"field_name":"postal_code","data":"90210"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * data_extraction_custom: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around custom fields
Example for data_extraction_custom: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked around 'What is going wrong (leak, no heat, clog, etc.).', user provided their information similar to [\"Water heater leaking\",\"Furnace won't start\"], that is valid and extracted","data_extracted":[{"unique_id":"cf_issue","data":"Water heater leaking"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.


 ### Tools Available:
- * data_extraction_custom: Extract the data for the custom fields as per the field description
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.
### When to Use Tools:
- * data_extraction_custom: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around custom fields
Example for data_extraction_custom: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked around 'The classified type of issue. Derived by the bot from the conversation; not asked as a direct question.', user provided their information similar to [\"Billing\",\"Bug\",\"How-to\"], that is valid and extracted","data_extracted":[{"unique_id":"cf_category","data":"Billing"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.

- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.

- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.

- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.


 ### Tools Available:
- * data_extraction_standard: Extract the data for the standard fields as per the field description
- * data_extraction_custom: Extract the data for the custom fields as per the field description
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.
### When to Use Tools:
- * data_extraction_standard: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around standard fields
Example for data_extraction_standard: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked for postal_code, user provided their information, which is valid and hence extracted","data_extracted":[{"field_name":"postal_code","data":"90210"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * data_extraction_custom: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around custom fields
Example for data_extraction_custom: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked around 'What is going wrong (leak, no heat, clog, etc.).', user provided their information similar to [\"Water heater leaking\",\"Furnace won't start\"], that is valid and extracted","data_extracted":[{"unique_id":"cf_issue","data":"Water heater leaking"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.


 ### Tools Available:
- * data_extraction_custom: Extract the data for the custom fields as per the field description
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.
### When to Use Tools:

Example for data_extraction_custom: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked around 'The community name the prospect types, captured verbatim. Do not correct spelling.', user provided their information similar to [\"the one on Oak\",\"Maplewood\"], that is valid and extracted","data_extracted":[{"unique_id":"cf_prop_raw","data":"the one on Oak"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}

DEA prompt
You are a data extraction agent. You are given a conversation between a user and an assistant. You need to extract the data from the conversation.

## Questions Mapping from the user's System prompt:
[
  { "field": "Issue Description", "Question": "Can you tell me what's happening?" },
  { "field": "Emergency Status", "Question": "Is this an emergency that needs someone today, or can it wait for a scheduled visit?" },
  { "field": "Service Address", "Question": "What's the address we're coming to?; What's the address for the visit?" },
  { "field": "Service Area", "Question": "Which town or area is that in?; What town or area is that?" },
  { "field": "full_name", "Question": "Who should the technician ask for on arrival?; And whose name should the appointment be under?" },
  { "field": "phone", "Question": "What's the best cell number in case the tech needs to call on the way?" },
  { "field": "postal_code", "Question": "What's your ZIP code so we can confirm you're in our coverage?" },
  { "field": "Preferred Appointment Window", "Question": "What time window works best for you?" }
]

### Conversation:
User: "It's 42 Elm Street, the clog is in the kitchen on the first floor."
---
Assistant: "Thanks. What town or area is that?"
---
User: "That's in Bellevue."
---
Assistant: "Perfect. What time window works best for you?"
---
User: "Tomorrow morning would be great."
---
Assistant: "Got it. What's your ZIP code so we can confirm you're in our coverage?"
---
User: "98004"
---
Assistant: "And whose name should the appointment be under?"
---
User: "Put it under Marcus."
---
Assistant: "All set, Marcus. We'll confirm your tomorrow-morning window shortly. Thanks for calling BlueFlame!"

### Important Guidelines:
- Extract a field **only** if the assistant explicitly asks one of the questions listed for that field in the mapping table **and** the user directly answers that question in the conversation.
- You can extract information for various fields in the data_extracted array, ensuring each field is extracted only once.
- Extract a field only if the immediately preceding assistant message exactly equals the mapped question (case-insensitive, punctuation-insensitive). Otherwise, do not extract
- DO NOT infer, assume or derive values from the context.
- Do not include fields with null, undefined, or empty string values.
- Only extract the valid information,
  * What is valid information?
    1. All the fields extracted should be of valid as per the examples according to respective tools
    2. All the fields extracted should be present in the conversation and are being talked about
- If no data can be extracted under these rules, use the 'indicate_no_extraction_needed' tool and provide a reason.


 ### Tools Available:
- * data_extraction_standard: Extract the data for the standard fields as per the field description
- * data_extraction_custom: Extract the data for the custom fields as per the field description
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: This is en escape tool to avoid extracting wrong information.
### When to Use Tools:
- * data_extraction_standard: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around standard fields
Example for data_extraction_standard: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked for postal_code, user provided their information, which is valid and hence extracted","data_extracted":[{"field_name":"postal_code","data":"90210"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * data_extraction_custom: Trigger when in the conversation between an assistant and a user, user provided information around custom fields
Example for data_extraction_custom: {"reasoning":"in the conversation, assistant asked around 'What is going wrong (leak, no heat, clog, etc.).', user provided their information similar to [\"Water heater leaking\",\"Furnace won't start\"], that is valid and extracted","data_extracted":[{"unique_id":"cf_issue","data":"Water heater leaking"}]}
Above example is just for reference. Do not copy or use these values unless the user has provided them for this field in this conversation
- * indicate_no_extraction_needed: Trigger this tool if you don't need to extract any data from the user.
Example for indicate_no_extraction_needed: {"reason":"User did not provide any relevant information"}
